Things might seem confusing and tough to understand, but keep reading and exploring. Remember, blockchain's holy grail is creating a decentralized and secure network with a high transaction-per-second rate. Achieving this requires developing sophisticated mechanisms, such as implementing rollups with zero-knowledge proofs and fault-proof systems.

22/05/2024, 21:01 - anurag: Hey all, Just a high-level overview of the BootCamp; as most of the boot campers here are beginners to blockchain, we decided to revamp the BootCamp. 
- The first 3 weeks take you through blockchain advancements and end by introducing zero knowledge and rust. 
- From week 4 onwards, we will dive into zero-knowledge, learn the basics, and code a few zero-knowledge systems.
This decision is made keeping everyone's interests first, so most of you feel the purpose of learning zero knowledge (tho zero knowledge is not limited to blockchain). 

If you are really interested to begin with zero knowledge then my DM's are open.
22/05/2024, 21:01 - anurag: cargo is a package manager to rust, similar to what npm is for node.js , package.json is equivalent to cargo.toml here in rust, more about cargo here https://doc.rust-lang.org/cargo/

22/05/2024, 21:01 - anurag: The Minutes of Meet today:
1. installed Rust and added extension - Rust analyzer
2. written first lines in rust(1.2) - understood how compiled languages work unlike others
3. understood what cargo does(1.3) - Cargo.toml, src, files generated using cargo build, and why cargo check and cargo run
4. created a guessing game - in this we understood libraries like io and Rand, crates, mutability of strings, ok and Err variants of Result and ordering, matching, error handling using expect if not rust panics, methods like parse(), trim(), expect(), loop and break.
5. Rust resources - Lets Get Rusty playlist, The Rust book(brown university version with quizzes), Rust by example, Rustlings
General Recommendation: Learn Rust from Day 0.
(https://doc.rust-lang.org/stable/book/) - The Rust Book
https://rust-book.cs.brown.edu/ - rust book with more detailed explanation and quizzes
(https://youtu.be/OX9HJsJUDxA?si=1xtatEZ4VTrEzKu5) - Let's Get Rusty Playlist
(https://doc.rust-lang.org/rust-by-example/index.html) - Rust by Example
(https://github.com/rust-lang/rustlings) - Rustlings
22/05/2024, 21:01 - anurag: Resources for the topics covered in today's session
rollups - https://vitalik.eth.limo/general/2021/01/05/rollup.html
Scaling Ethereum - https://youtu.be/zADuI0a1c9A?si=VfJ3wIiglXxX70Zc
slides - https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/15lxDiJm_Rz5BeFzPxfFwfbys-OWgvtMXXkrBJSA2_Yk/edit#slide=id.g2b8fcc687c3_0_9
eip4844 - https://github.com/ethereum/EIPs/blob/master/EIPS/eip-4844.md 
Things might seem confusing and tough to understand, but keep reading and exploring. Remember, blockchain's holy grail is creating a decentralized and secure network with a high transaction-per-second rate. Achieving this requires developing sophisticated mechanisms, such as implementing rollups with zero-knowledge proofs and fault-proof systems.
